padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2319718" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="venussiandehermes"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2107198"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2107198.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="venussiandehermes" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Gisada/Ambassador-Intense-76636.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.76636.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Ambassador Intense"title="Ambassador Intense"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2319718ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2319718" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.8); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2107198">venussiandehermes</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-18">10/18/24 08:15</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A wonderfully easy to wear perfume. Suitable for wearing day and night in all conditions and almost every season. Only on very hot summer days its sweetness can be a bit overwhelming. But it looks great for summer evenings.<br />
<br />
The combination of apple, cardamom and lavender notes in Layton was probably used for the first time in this perfume as it is used here. Add to this the perfume's harmony that suits general taste, and this perfume has become so popular. It seems that icons like Layton responded to the Aventus wave of the early 2010s at PDM. Of course, Layton and Aventus have nothing to do with each other in terms of scent similarity. But in terms of perfumes that are open to general taste, the simultaneity of Layton and Aventus in the niche perfume community made this association to me.<br />
<br />
There is a strong menthol air in the opening of the perfume. When I first sprayed it on my arm, I said: is this the Layton that everyone is exaggerating? Huh. But after a few minutes I started to smell a very classy, sophisticated scent. This scent is really popular and stands out from the sweet scents that are popular at this time with its quality. Although the scent profile reminds me of something I've tried for the first time, it has a very interesting atmosphere, just like in niche perfumes. You can tell that this perfume is niche from the quality of the scent. This is the general impression I get from PDM perfumes in general. This perfume house makes fragrances that suit general tastes. It seems that PDM's success has begun to be replicated by other niche perfume houses. The gap between niche and designer perfumes released today is gradually closing.<br />
<br />
I think Latyon is a perfume suitable for blind buying. But the rumors that PDM's current batches are weaker than the old ones seem to be true. I was not very satisfied with the performance of all my PDMs except Kalan. However, this recommendation is not based on long-term experience. I only tried it in a perfume store. I am very pleased with the performance of my Percival, Pegasus and Layton.<br />
What I'm trying to say is: I recommend you don't buy Layton without trying its performance. There doesn't seem to be a problem with the scent in terms of general liking.<br />
<br />
Whether you are a collector or someone who prefers to own just one or a few perfumes, Layton is a perfume that truly deserves to be tried.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Unfortunately, it left me feeling quite underwhelmed. While the fragrance opens with a pleasant blend of apple, bergamot, and spices, the initial burst quickly fades, leaving behind a scent that is, at best, mediocre.<br />
<br />
One of my biggest issues with Layton is its lack of projection and longevity. For a fragrance with such a high price point, I expected something that would last throughout the day, but it barely lingered for a few hours before fading away. It just doesn’t have the power I was hoping for, making it feel weak and uninspiring.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="2319319"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=2319319#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2318493" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I've found it too straight, there is no tension, no sublime. This perfume is like a golden Rolex - people who like it believe it's peak horlogerie and wealth.<br />
<br />
I am not even a perfume snob, I enjoy Creed Aventus for goodness sake!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="2318171"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=2318171#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2316697" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2311570" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="NuclearAquaticsWanted"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2282796"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="NuclearAquaticsWanted" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2311570ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2311570" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.74); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2282796">NuclearAquaticsWanted</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-10">10/10/24 15:50</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Favourite. Fragrance. Ever.<br />
<br />
Like many men in their late 20s or early 30s, I thought I had found the ultimate scent when I discovered Aventus. Then, I stumbled upon Layton — and everything changed.<br />
<br />
Layton has truly been life-changing for me. I didn’t know a fragrance could smell this good.<br />
<br />
I seem to pick up notes in Layton that others don’t. For me, it’s all about this beautifully crafted chocolate note. It’s rich, sweet, and luxurious, with hints of dark cacao seed. I’m honestly surprised cacao isn’t listed as an official note on Fragrantica.<br />
<br />
In terms of performance, Layton is a beast. It projects strongly for at least four hours, then settles into a luxurious skin scent for another six. I can spray it on in the morning, go to work, get compliments from colleagues throughout the day, and still get praised by my wife when I get home — all from just four sprays.<br />
<br />
It’s also a sillage monster and perfect for a night out. I’ve had three separate compliments in one night while wearing it at a club. Yet, unlike many mass-appeal scents, Layton never becomes boring. It’s complex, warm, and feels like wrapping your hands around a cup of rich Austrian hot chocolate on a cold winter evening.<br />
<br />
Layton is a masterpiece, and I can’t imagine it being topped.<br />
<br />
I have a sample of Layton Exclusif sitting on my shelf and will do a review of that soon!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="2311570"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=2311570#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2311330" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Rock solid everywhere and my favorite scent in Fall or Winter easily.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="2311330"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=2311330#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2309218" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2308359" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="ISmellGood93"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1832728"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1832728.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="ISmellGood93" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Ombre-Leather-2018-50239.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.50239.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Ombré Leather (2018)"title="Ombré Leather (2018)"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2308359ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2308359" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1832728">ISmellGood93</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-07">10/07/24 20:04</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Writing a seperate review of this as my first was just too long. <br />
<br />
This community is wild af... For one, now, I admit that batch variations have happened with this, its pretty plain to see, different packaging, different concentration, but for most of you to claim this lasts 30 minutes - 4 hours tops is some of the biggest bullshit I've read on this site so far. This seems to be a trend on this website right now especially. You can see this crap on almost every frag, but right now, its like the crack is extra strong. Not to mention, if a brand releases a flanker, or god for bid you don't like the perfumer, these that shit on batch variations like this, have GOT to be the same idiots that immediately flock to new frags and instantly hit the hate button, give it shit ratings on performance and leave before the new frag even hits the store. Shame on yall that have shat on this, and really that shit on everything else too. Genuinely. The last like 4-6 reviews I've written I've had to call out these stupid people that either got something fake, or just are so hooked on that batch number on the bottom on the box, are asnomic as shit, or have literally horrible skin and need to see a dermatologist. Idk what it is.....<br />
<br />
Moving forward. Layton, contrary to the current popular belief amongst what seems to be at least half of the recent reviewers here, has not only been one of the most intoxicating beautiful fragrances I've ever purchased, but I can happily let anyone know that if they're worried about the performance because of reviews, don't worry about it. It's great. Thankfully for me I've never smelled an old batch of this or anything of the sort, so I got this completely unbiased, going in having never smelled this at all. <br />
<br />
I managed to track down a tester in a beautiful fragrance shop and was immediately blown away by this on a tester. I reacted the same way I did to Sauvage Elixir, knowing immediately I had to have this. It opens with a slightly medicinal vibe, nothing I dislike, I actually find it incredibly beautiful. Hard to line up what I smell here with what is listed as the notes. I could see "apple pie" a little bit. But to me, I really get a beautiful tobacco vibe, washed in lavender, and as crazy as it sounds, It's almost like they had some kind of licorice note similar to Sauvage Elixir (though this came out years before DSE), but they took this and made it a totally different vibe and smell entirely from DSE, the two smell nothing alike, but I can't help but notice this note there. I've bought Mancera, but this is my first "high end" niche buy, and so maybe my nose just isn't trained as well for this stuff, because its a full level above anything I've bought thus far. From there, it settles into a beautiful vanilla with much of the same opening notes sticking around. It's incredibly warm and spicy, with a nice vanilla. Quality was not missed in this blend. A masterpiece in my eyes, and it would seem many other folks as well... Intoxicating and addicting. <br />
<br />
Longevity is NOT what most reviewers are claiming here. Before purchase I came here to check out the reviews and spent the better part of 40 minutes trying to make up my mind, purely because a lot of you have claimed 30 minutes, up to 4 hours of total performance from this, which for me was very upsetting. But after a test spray on my wrist, I just knew I had to have this, I trusted my gut and the few good folks on this site giving adequate reviews, and snagged the 4.2oz bottle for only $225, which beat out every discounter I looked at but one, which had it for 220. So a win all in all there I think, the batch code is 3142541 and was made in I think it was april or march of 2023. RIGHT in the prime spot I see ALL the shitty reviewers chiming from. It has the new box, that no longer has the striped blue and white. Just a solid blue, and I shit you not, I was getting light sillage up to 22 hours before I showered off the sprays from yesterday. I am now 10 hours into a full wearing as I write this, and it continues its relatively strong to moderate sillage everytime I move at all. DO NOT believe the bullshit people are spewing about the longevity. They are wrong, I promise :)<br />
<br />
Sillage is pretty great all in all, very impressed that its strong for 5-6 hours before getting a little more moderate but still strong. This didn't really tame down for me until around the 13 hour mark, but I could still detect it from almost a foot away the next morning waking up. <br />
<br />
So idk. This rates up with every review that I read here, from youtube, from reddit, from reviews on discounters that were from before 2021 (funnily enough, lots of the same snobs claiming shit performance from this it would appear going back to 2018 which is as far as I scrolled reading), and it rates up with every review that I've seen that doesn't mention that batch variation and then proceeds to shit on the performance, or just blatantly shitting on its performance in general, that are from after 2021. I call bullshit on anyone saying this isn't good. It has held up to the exact standard it seemed to be held at before that "precious" batch change. So I'm not only incredibly happy with this, but I'm glad I got the big bottle. :D<br />
<br />
Edit because i thought this was funny: I couldn't help but think about this as I'm waking up today, but if this was SO much stronger 2 years ago, wouldn't that be a bad thing for you snobs? Most of yall are these "more than 2 sprays of anything is ABSURD" people that will wear 2 splashes of old spice and bitch that in 30 minutes it's gone, but then someone gives you a high power chemical bomb of a frag (this is AFTER reformulation, so i can only imagine if it really was THAT much stronger before), and you bitch when they reformulate it to where your 2 sprays for the day are now just nuclear, instead of chemical warfare. You should be happy about that. Not bitching about it. As an oversprayer, I shouldn't be happy about it, but I am. Shit is backwards.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="2308359"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=2308359#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2307940" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />

Smells wonderful and the performance is great. I don't care much for PDM as a whole but this frag is top tier.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="2307940"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=2307940#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2306352" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; PDM did a great job being a niche quality mass appealer.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="2288643"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=2288643#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2288394" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1647189">dayonee</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-18">09/18/24 16:24</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Due to its popularity, I've always been curious about Layton. Tried it a few times on a tester strip but didn't really win me over. But that curiosity got me to get a bottle at a reasonable price. One can say that it was a half blind buy, since I've never tried it on skin, but I knew it wasn't going to be a complete bust either. <br />
<br />
That Vick's Vapor rub/menthol smell is present but, for me, very short-lived right after the initial spray. Fresh apple scent is dominant well into the drydown, where it is met with a semi sweet vanillia. More for cooler weather but fresh enough to be worn during late spring/early fall. Tried Detour Noir in the past but this is MUCH smoother and well done; yes, they smell similar but the quality is miles apart. Masculine and well put. Fantastic perfume, overall.<br />
<br />
Is it worth the retail? My philosophy has always been, if you like it and have the means, go for it. I personally think anything over $200 for a perfume is bonkers. (only perfume I have paid retail over that amount is LV Imagination because I love the scent) But if you like it enough to pay, either retail or discounted, you won't regret getting this. EXCELLENT.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="2287405"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=2287405#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2286946" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2282796" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="ZeaMoore4"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1761519"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1761519.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="ZeaMoore4" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.39314.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Layton"title="Layton"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2282796ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2282796" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.73); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1761519">ZeaMoore4</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-14">09/14/24 12:51</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>There should be a warning label on every Layton bottle: "Warning. Gateway Fragrance! Wear only when designer fragrances have become boring to you".<br />
<br />
The first time i tried something other than "designer" and "cheapies", was a bottle of PDM Layton. At that point, i had about 25-30 designers and cheap fragrances (clones), and life was cheap and easy. Every spray could be wasted, as they didn't cost much, and i had plenty. I had heard about some "magic" fragrance called "Layton" that would spellbind everyone around me, get me laid 250 times per hour, i would become emperor of the world and aliens would travel here from other dimensions just to kiss my feet and sniff my neck.... Of course this was back when i trusted random people on the internet, that made a living selling me fake dreams and false promises. Then at a later time, someone serious actually told me about Layton, and i thought: "He sounds smarter then all the weird YouTube people with top 10 lists". So i checked it out. <br />
<br />
The first sniff was amazing. A little strong and kind of menthol ish. My untrained nose struggled to grasp the nuances in the scent. There is so much i can pick out. Vanilla, obviously. But also a fresh apple, lavender, something spicy and familiar. Cardamom? Yes, that's it. my eyes widened, my heart raced, my head hurt a little. This was a whole other world!<br />
<br />
To this day, it's still a journey through notes and accords. But now, after 2 years of exploring hundreds of niche fragrances and even more designers. I Always come back to Layton thinking: "You cost me a Lot of money". I was happy smelling like a cheap Aventus clone or CK ONE. Now i consider Creed Aventus to be boring and generic, and i wouldn't wear CK ONE if it was the last fragrance on earth. My friends smirk and tell me i'm "wasting my money", as they themselves waste their money on other dumb shit😅.<br />
<br />
Here's the short of it: PDM Layton is a gateway drug... fragrance, and will 100% be loved by a Lot of people around you. Maybe even by yourself. It's worthy of a sample at the very least. Full bottle for most. If you get it, get the 125ml bottle. You'll never stop wearing it, it gets better with age (if stored correctly) and you can always sell the bottle if you don't wear it for some reason. <br />
<br />
Autumn/Winter/spring, day and night, casual, formal, date night and hitting the night clubs. Any age, leaning heavy masculine but some ladies pull it of. <br />
<br />
Personal score: 9.75/10. It's Almost as good as my two favorite fragrances of all time. Almost.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="2282796"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=2282796#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2281906" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I see some people compare it with Xerjoff Naxos and I can see that, however Naxos is a much more pleasing scent, from the first minute to the ending, unlike Layton where you have to give it a few minutes. Performance is pretty good, with about 7 hours longevity, mid projection. <br />
<br />
I don't get the apple pie that people are saying though. I get mostly that cardamom and lavender, with a touch of vanilla. If you want to smell like an apple pie just go get Khamrah Qawah Lattafa.<br />
<br />
After all being said that doesn't mean it smells bad. Smells pretty good, and would be a good crowd pleasing scent. I just don't think it will justify the price.<br />
<br />
Scent: 4/5<br />
Longevity: 4/5<br />
Price 2/5<br />
<br />
3.3/5</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="2274780"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=2274780#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2274434" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Get Carlisle, Haltane, Althair or  Herod.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="2274201"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=2274201#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2273843" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2273843" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Nefster84"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1976630"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1976630.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Nefster84" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Afnan/Supremacy-Not-Only-Intense-68271.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.68271.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Supremacy Not Only Intense"title="Supremacy Not Only Intense"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2273843ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2273843" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1976630">Nefster84</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-06">09/06/24 12:01</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Let’s address the elephant in the room. Menthol is the main note when you first spray it on. If you don’t like menthol you probably won’t like this. After a few minutes you get the apple with some florals. The lavender and geranium give it a cool fresh feel. I do get a sweeter apple and spice smell when sprayed on clothes. Also the vanilla, cardamom, and sandalwood give it warmth, sweet powdery comfort. I do enjoy moving around and catching the scent in the air. This projects really good for like 3 hours, sillage is good and you will leave a scent trail. Longevity is great. I still smell this 12 hours later. <br />
<br />
Does it smell good? Yes.<br />
Does it last? Yes  <br />
Does it project? Yes<br />
Is it worth the price? Depends. Get a sample and try it. I sampled this first but that one didn’t have as strong menthol smell as my full bottle. I will say I smell the menthol less the more I wear it so it could take a little getting used to. I like it but won’t be repurchasing. <br />
<br />
I have Herod and sample of Carlisle and honestly I prefer those over this.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="2273843"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=2273843#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2273137" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; If you like it, buy off a discounter. 6/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="2260604"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=2260604#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2258131" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; This scent captures attention and admiration with its sweet and spicy aroma, making it both inviting and irresistible. It's best worn in cooler weather, shining in fall and winter, and is ideal for evening occasions and nights out. Layton works well for various events, from casual to formal, exuding confidence and strength.Though it comes with a high price point, the quality justifies the cost.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; I am in the seemingly small minority who is just NOT impressed with Layton. Im not saying this to "go against the grain" or to "troll" or be a "lame ass hater" just bc of this fragrance's popularity.<br />
<br />
After hearing ALL THE HYPE I was convinced that I would like Layton, but I was concerned that I would end up smelling like everyone else (I still do not own Sauvage or any of the clones for that reason) but figured I would atleast try a dupe just to see if Id like the dna. I ordered Leyden by Lattafa, when I got it and sprayed it on while standing next to my brother, both our eyes widened bc it smelled just like an Avon perfume called Mesmerize that released about 30 years ago! <br />
<br />
I was cinvinced Id recieved one of those weird counterfeit Lattafas that have been going around,  so I went to the mall and tried PDM Leyden, and yep, it smelled JUST LIKE MESMERIZE. I was shocked to say the least and really hope folks start trying Mesmerize which is still available on Walmart.com.<br />
<br />
 I never liked Mesmerize so thats why I dont like PDM's Leyden. Smells like a vintage fougere and older gentleman would wear imo, not my speed. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1874308">Porobear</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-01">08/01/24 02:55</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Yeah, it's Layton. There are probably more reviews on Layton than there are on most designer fragrances. So you know  what people have been saying about it. Is it worth the hype?<br />
Yes and no. <br />
<br />
It's a pretty versatile and mass appealing scent. And although the recent formulations are a bit worse than the older ones (things have been changed due to new EU regulations), it's still a good scent. It's well blended and rounded, has a great vanilla in it that reveals itself later on and the apple lavender combo still slaps.<br />
<br />
I personally enjoy Oajan a bit more, as that one fully commits to the apple pie with its cinnamon, but I recognise that Oajan is a bit more unwearable because of it.<br />
<br />
8.5/10.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="2235420"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=2235420#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2233509" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; This is vanilla and apple done in a bad way, if you've ever smelled scandal by jpg you'll know what I mean, it's a bad combination of fruity and warm sweet notes<br />
<br />
I'm not saying it's bad, what I am saying is that there are videos asking people on the street if they preferred Layton or a 3 dollar Adidas cologne and the Adidas won.<br />

However, this is for good reason. The scent is very good. The fragrance opens with green apple and vanilla with a little bit of spices and woods. The fragrance is very sooth and creamy. To me, the scent does not change all that much throughout its life. The scent is sweet but nothing overpowering. I do enjoy this much more than Layton exclusif but that is due to the overpowering almond in exclusif. <br />
<br />
This fragrance can be worn in pretty much any occasion during winter, fall, and spring. I would not recommend wearing this during the summer except for at night. This is a very good beginner niche that is very mass appealing. Some complain about the performance but i think it performs very good. 12+ hours longevity with 6+ hours with great projection. <br />
<br />
Longevity: 9/10<br />
Projection: 8/10<br />
Smell: 10/10<br />
Price: 8/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="2218308"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=2218308#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2217637" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1322412">Sajjad_Frag</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-02">07/02/24 12:45</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Overall rating (9/10)<br />
<br />
Layton by Parfums de Marly is a fragrance that earns high praise for its captivating and complex scent. This scent captures attention and admiration with its sweet and spicy aroma, making it both inviting and irresistible. It's best worn in cooler weather, shining in fall and winter, and is ideal for evening occasions and nights out. Layton works well for various events, from casual to formal, exuding confidence and strength. Though it comes with a high price point, the quality justifies the cost.<br />
<br />
Ratings:<br />
- Longevity: Lasts for 7-9 hours (8/10)<br />
- Projection: Radiates well for the first 1-2 hours (7/10)<br />
- Scent: Perfect blend of sweetness and spiciness (10/10)<br />
- Material Quality: Reflects its premium price with top-notch ingredients (10/10)<br />
<br />
Overall, Layton by Parfums de Marly is a sophisticated and luxurious fragrance that stands out in any collection. Its high-quality ingredients, well-balanced composition, and captivating scent make it a perfect choice for those seeking a versatile and masculine fragrance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2160902">J_Resinanxce</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-26">06/26/24 03:00</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This fragrance is the definition of overhyped and overpriced. Sure, it is a very pleasant spicy fruity/vanilla scent, but it really isnt anything special or original. The opening is super alcoholic for me, gave me an instant headache since it smelt like menthol lozenges. Additionally, the projection is not as good as described, although longevity is quite excellent getting about 7-11 hours on skin. <br />
<br />
In conclusion, it is a pleasant dry down scent, and performance is unquestionable, but there are so many fragrances out there that are cheaper, have the same Layton DNA and ultimately smell better. Although, if you have $460 lying around, and you just want a frag that makes the girls fall in love, Layton might be a good option. Tbh, this review leans nor negative nor postive, it is all opinion based after all.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="2199772"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=2199772#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2197684" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1445544">jbozz</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-21">06/21/24 09:20</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Ahhh, Layton. I know it's hyped but there's just something about it that hits all the right spots with me, and there's a reason that it gets all the attention that it does. It really has a beautiful balance of fresh spicy, warm spicy, sweet and ever so slightly gourmand (like a homemade apple pie á la mode). This is not for fragrance connoisseurs looking for some groundbreaking scent. This is niche for the masses and it's done exceptionally well in my opinion. It totally has an autumn vibe going on but it's also versatile enough that it can wear it almost any time except warm/hot weather. I love getting wafts of it and gives me such a cozy feeling. On my skin all the notes are just blended so smoothly and it all meshes together wonderfully. Ingredients smell high quality as usual with PDM. I have a newer bottle from a 2023 batch and the menthol note is GONE, and I don't get any of that vapo rub smell that so many get. Performance is<br />
respectable about 7+ hours and it easily lasts on clothes into the next day. Just a lovely scent and it's understandable that it gets mad hype. And just speaking for myself, but I could easily have just Layton and Percival from this house and not need any other fragrances. For spring/summer (Percival) and autumn/winter (Layton). Just these two could cover all the ground I'd ever need.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="2195164"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=2195164#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2193533" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1043744">FreshLiving</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-19">06/19/24 16:59</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I’ve been diving in to Parfums de Marley full bore for the last two weeks. I’ve sampled all of their current website men’s listings. <br />
<br />
Layton is an exceptional fragrance. It’s does everything all at once. It’s incredible. I understand the hype and the craze here.<br />
If I could only have three fragrances for the rest of my life, this would be on it, since it really is a jack of all trades scent. <br />
It’s comforting, complex, sexy, spicy, warm, fresh, dressy, classy, masculine, alluring.<br />
<br />
I hunted down and ordered a 2018 batch and it arrived today. Its projection and scent is great. <br />
As for the Vicks scent that people are talking about, I really don’t get much of that at all. Mine opens up spicy, but in a fresh way. Nowhere near VapoRub though; I feel that is sinply internet echo chamber going full tilt as per usual when it comes to fragrances. One person says it and then others just parrot. <br />
<br />
Anyways, I tried the new batch from my sample on one hand and 2018 bottle on the other, and there is a difference aside from the menthol note. The older version is much more dense. The new is more airy my but still delightful. More apple off the top.<br />
<br />
Fantastic fragrance overall. Great house, can’t wait for my 5 other PdM’s to arrive now!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="2193533"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=2193533#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2192937" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2192937" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="D. <br />
I like Layton, it's a vanilla-centric scent supported by light fruity and spicy notes with a touch of floral and woody quality. I'm positively surprised to find a not too sweet/heavy kind of scent, as that was my primary concern. I'm not having much of that balsamic note that many reviews mention, stil it's got a fresh undertone that lifts the perfume profile.<br />
<br />
Very well crafted, clean, approachable, palatable, lingers for 10+ hours, I can see how this is so popular. However, this is far from being a groundbreaking niche fragrance, it's actually a pretty safe one. Suitable for all seasons except high heat conditions.<br />
<br />

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2190903" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Zac_Saffron"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2167161"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2167161.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Zac_Saffron" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Haltane-70776.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.70776.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Haltane"title="Haltane"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2190903ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2190903" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2167161">Zac_Saffron</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-17">06/17/24 08:53</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Story time: <br />
So prior to having ever smelled this for the first time in January, I was only ever exposed to designer fragrances (like the vast majority of the population). I didn’t know what niche fragrances were or the concept and theory behind them were either. At least in my region, 95% of the people here give a shit less about perfumes and colognes. <br />
<br />
But as I started diving further into fragrances as a hobby and collector, Parfums de Marly was introduced to me by almost every perfume reviewer and “influencer” on YouTube who spoke so highly of Layton from this niche house. Every ‘Top 10’ video had it in their list. Top 10 fragrances for the fall, Top 10 colognes to make women wet, Top 10 niche scents that smell like you wipe your ass with $100 bills. It was put on a pedestal as this holy grail of fragrances. Several months later when I finally had a chance to get my nose on a fresh tester strip it was at Dallas Fort Worth international airport and let me just say, it was not at all what I was expecting…<br />
<br />
If you’re someone like me who’s only ever known popular and trendy fragrances from popular and trendy designer brands, the first time smelling something niche like Layton will punch you in the teeth and tackle you to the floor. My nose wasn’t prepared for the assault on my senses. <br />
<br />
You’re immediately slapped with a strong minty Vic’s VapoRub menthol scent (this is subjective, not everyone gets that smell but I did) followed by a faint apple note with vanilla. I initially did not like this scent, but as time went on I couldn’t stop thinking about it and I had to test it on skin next. And just like our sense of tastes change over time, so does our sense of smells. And now as of June Layton smells magical to me and I finally understand the appeal presented by the fragrance community. Needless to say I bought myself a full 125ml bottle and love every spray. <br />
<br />
Layton is a fantastic fragrance but you need time to develop an understanding and appreciation for it. If you’re a fragrance newby dipping your toes into niche like me, I think it’s a good rule of thumb that you start out small and TEST TEST TEST everything and anything that piques your interest.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; It smells good on the opening and in the bottle, but on my skin, I do not enjoy this. The mix of candy apple and spices is just extremely meh; it almost feels like it's trying too hard to be unique. I felt similarly about Hawas, but in hotter weather, Hawas evolves into something fairly enjoyable, at least combining with my body oils. However with this, as soon as I go outside in the hot weather and start smelling the sillage of my skin and this mixing, I am almost inclined to lean away from it. It's too heavy on the warm spiciness to mix well with the fruit and florals, on my skin and in my local climate. Maybe this is way better in cold weather situations, will have to test further in a few months.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="2182707"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=2182707#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2182596" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2101926">ke3ke3</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-02">06/02/24 15:44</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Personally, I love this fragrance. I only own a sample, but I've just ordered a full bottle. Initially, my plan had been to gift this to my father for Christmas, but as I've been testing it myself, I don't know if I can let it go! I've read through the comments and I don't see anyone mentioning this fragrance on women - to me, it's very unisex. That was my initial concern in gifting it to my father, he tends to like very masculine colognes and to me, this is not that! But of course, I see that I am very much in the minority in my opinion. But still, it is my opinion that this is a unsiex fragrance, slightly masculine leaning.<br />
<br />
This seems like something that could be worn year-round, at least on a man. For me, it's something I would wear during the fall and winter! I am not getting syrupy at all, to me the bergamot is what's standing out the most. I find this fragrance to be very crisp and pleasant. I was not aware that it's so polarizing! To me, it seems very safe.... As much as I'd prefer not to, I would agree with the comments that this is a designer fragrance at a niche price. As much as I love Parfums de Marly, this seems to be true for a lot of this house.<br />
<br />
I very much love this fragrance! I think it's fairly priced, if you can find it in stock on certain websites. The full asking price to me, feels unjustified. I was able to pick up a full-size bottle for less than half of the MSRP! Time will tell if I can bare to part with it... until then, I will continue enjoying my sample!! Noting that the sample came from a very trusted and well-known decanter, so there is no concern as to whether it could be fake or not... It seems like I often perceive fragrances a bit differently than others, which, is okay! But clarifying that my review is indeed of genuine Layton.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="2175965"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=2175965#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2175612" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Projection 8/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="2175234"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=2175234#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2175161" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Always has been. And the legend only grows. <br />
<br />
It is a Niche priced designer fragrance that is heavy vanillic, and apple. The opening is dreadful to me, the mid is much better, but you can buy vanilla/ warm spice based scents all over the market. I don't see the slight apple note being worth the price tag.<br />
<br />
JMHO to each their own, just don't blind buy this. Same as with any fragrance, really. The everlasting hype train may not stop at your house.<br />
<br />

It's thick, syrupy vanilla, tends to be cloying.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="2174811"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=2174811#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2174596" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I bought this scent a while back before all this tik tok hype, even before all the fragrance hype on social media. To me Layton is a very vanilla heavy scent, with a slight scent of that apple note. There’s a bit of spices and woodiness jn there but in whole it’s a vanilla heavy scent. And I do really love this scent, but it’s not extremely unique. However, it’s crazy longevity and projection help this stand out. It smells amazing, it’s perfect for date nights and honestly any outting in my opinion. Great for that winter fall season. It’s a very likable and very complimented scent. There isn’t anything too negative to say about Layton. This scent was played safe yet still manages to be good and is between the typical designer and niche fragrances. However, st that price point I do think you can pickup more unique fragrances. And I do think Althair is a better alternative at the same price which is also quiet like able. But at the end of the day, Layton is just an amazing scent and a top 5 de Marley fragrance.<br />

Projection: 8<br />
Longevity: 10<br />
Value: 7<br />

It has sandalwood and lavender which helps make it more masculine. To me it smells like vanilla ice cream, the soft stuff with the little black dots in it. The creamy lavender dry down is amazing and I do not particularly enjoy the smell of lavender. <br />
<br />
This scent lasts for very long and projects extremely well. The biggest drawback to this other than the price is the community. <br />
<br />
Parfums De Marley Layton has an almost cult following. It does smell a little synthetic and it does cause headaches. I love Layton, but don't let the reviews tell all the story!!! <br />
<br />
Your fragrance journey is yours to be explored, a comment section where everyone is close minded and praising a $400 bottle of alcohol and oil should not tell you anything about how you will like the fragrance. Get a sample of this and you won't regret it, even if you don't love it the same as the rest of us.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="2170997"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=2170997#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="39314" sentiment="all"></reviews-infinity>

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1005101" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="WhatAFrag"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1172168"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1172168.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="WhatAFrag" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1005101ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck8x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1005101" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.72); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1172168">WhatAFrag</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2018-11-28">11/28/18 23:12</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Let’s forget about both niche and designer categories for a second. We throw the word generic around much too often. Bleu De Chanel was extremely disliked by fragcom when it first released because it was too “generic.” They said it was generic and dated yet 8 years later it inspired many top sellers. Is something truly generic? Or is it just a phrase too over used in fragcom?<br />
<br />
Layton is in my opinion a brand new take into a masculine sweet fragrance. A borderline gourmand but with a fresh bite. A rich apple note with warm cinnamon with vanilla that’s aggressive, yet inviting. The opening does come off a bit like other openings of designer realms such as bergamot based openings but the scent is far from over. 15 minutes after you’ll start to detect the warm cinnamon and creamy sandalwood. I smell some rose in this somewhere in the heart, but not at all off putting. The apple in Layton is with the fragrance basically throughout the life of it. This is an amazing scent. <br />
<br />
The snobs will tell you this is generic and not even niche. But ask yourself this, when have you ever smelled something like Layton out there? There are other offerings from the house that indeed smell similar to designer fragrances. You can say Eros, ultra male, boss bottled, but none of those even come close to this creation. Do not pay attention to the niche snobs, you will smell like nobody in everyday life with this. Well done Parfums de Marly, you’ve done what most niche houses are afraid to do. And that’s make a crowd pleasing niche fragrance. Exclusif to my nose is wonderful but I prefer the sweetness of the original. If you’re into a woody or darker fragrance choose exclusif. <br />
<br />
<br />
I get 9+ hours on my skin with 5 hours of projection and a very nice complement getter<br />
<br />
<br />
9.5/10 this is my favorite offering from the house</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="1005101"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=1005101#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2197684" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
