padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/773120">Space</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2017-11-01">11/01/17 08:32</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A blob of generic notes, with none of them really standing out, except for the flat, bland vanilla and the overused herbal lavender. It smells cheap. I owned it, but got rid of it. Don't fall for the hype. This isn't a very good, nor well made fragrance. It's bad enough that I suspect the YouTube reviewers who push this stuff are being compensated for doing so.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="876158"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=876158#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1107948" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1107948" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="heartcooksbrain"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/601062"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.601062.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="heartcooksbrain" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Burberry/London-for-Men-804.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.804.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="London for Men"title="London for Men"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1107948ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck6x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1107948" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.82); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/601062">heartcooksbrain</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2019-10-19">10/19/19 15:59</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This fragrance has been given so much undeserved and misleading hype in my opinion. There's so much YouTube praise for it that I had to purchase a decant myself to see what the fuss was about. The initial spray really confused me. I immediately thought of a sharper, more piercing version of Mugler Pure Malt/Havane, and a rougher, more cloying dry down of Boss Bottled Intense EDP. I actually prefer both of those fragrances to this one. Boss Bottled Intense EDP has the vanilla/apple combo as well, but it's much smoother than this is. Layton does pack a lot of longevity though, but if I don't care for the scent as much as stuff I already have that are a fraction of the price, what's the point? It's not that Layton smells bad, but it's just too rough and cloying for me to thoroughly enjoy it. Definitely not a blind buy, and if I had purchased a bottle, I'd be splitting it out for sure.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="1107948"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=1107948#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1105492" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1105492" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Houdini4"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/607493"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.607493.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Houdini4" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Les-Indemodables/Vanille-Havane-Coeur-de-Oud-96892.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.96892.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Vanille Havane Coeur de Oud"title="Vanille Havane Coeur de Oud"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1105492ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1105492" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.86); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/607493">Houdini4</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2019-10-10">10/10/19 08:55</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I'm shocked that I never put pen to paper about this fragrance at the time I tried it (whenever that was?) Shocked because I actually thought this was a daft, bit of 'meh' that smelled vaguely of a apple, vanillic, musky haze and therefore pretty likable.<br />
<br />
I've subsequently worn it many times of the last few years (as I keep getting samples of the stuff!) desperately trying to understand the obvious 'bro' appeal  and I have to say that Layton ...is the devil. <br />
<br />
What a load of rubbish, I don't think I've ever had a scent do this, I mean grow worse and worse in my affections. It's initially okay I guess but soon becomes cloying and unfair to compare to Boss Bottled in reality. <br />
<br />
Actually I have had another do this... Mancera Cedrat Boise another popular but terrible fragrance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="1105492"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=1105492#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent917384" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc917384" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Benguin7"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/969300"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.969300.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Benguin7" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Patchouli-Absolu-28009.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.28009.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Patchouli Absolu"title="Patchouli Absolu"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma917384ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd917384" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.82); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/969300">Benguin7</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2018-03-02">03/02/18 04:37</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I'm still exploring this fresh-floral-spicy fragrance.  It has a vibrant, vaporous silage that add to it's effect.  As a sparkling, invigorating type of scent.  <br />
<br />
The thing that surprises me is that when I put my nose right on it, the apple-mandarin combo is good but not my favorite.  But when I smell the silage.  It blends all together beautifully.  <br />
<br />
The other thing that surprises me is the powerful compliments.  Not just nice ones, but strangely powerful ones.  <br />
<br />
A lady in an crowded elevator at work, leaned over and and exaggeratedly, breathed me in, and said, "Oh my god, you smell so delicious.." and we were both professionals there.  <br />
<br />
I had a couple people ask me what it was and then write it down.  <br />
<br />
So this one is more than just a pleasant crowd pleaser.  To me, at least.  It's some kind of powerful hypnotizing scent.  One that seems to please others more than me. <br />
<br />
I'm glad I got it.  It's a nice, versatile, 3-4 season scent.  With real attractive power.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="917384"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=917384#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1345301" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1345301" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="juliakatdavis"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1260583"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="juliakatdavis" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1345301ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1345301" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.83); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1260583">juliakatdavis</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-05-18">05/18/21 09:58</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I ordered a sample of this perfume and returned it because I thought it must be a mistake. This could not possibly be the scent that everyone on YouTube  was raving about. They sent me a new sample, and I was equally disappointed. Then I tested it out and Nordstrom to make sure… and yep. I just find this to be awful… cloyingly sweet and suffocating. Kind of like someone sprayed the cheapest possible hairspray and pepper spray into an incense store. Everyone else loves this, which is great. I’ve heard lots of great things about PDM. I just hope no one in my family or friend group discovers this scent because I couldn’t put up with it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39314"comment_id="1345301"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Layton-39314.html?ccid=1345301#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="39314" sentiment="negative"></reviews-infinity>
